································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································ God's Frustration

Everyone in the world tends to smile when they are happy and shed tears when they are sad. Ordinary people hope to live smiling, but we know through experience that our lives cannot be lived in laughter alone; that is the reality of life. Why is that? Living in laughter is close to happiness, while living in tears is close to unhappiness.

Finite humans cannot change the given environment.

When looking at this, if I ask you if you are happy, those who smile with joy will likely answer that they are happy. But can that happiness be guaranteed? The time spent smiling can easily turn into misery. On the other hand, if I ask a miserable person, someone who is crying, "Are you unhappy?" they will answer that they are unhappy. Now, how long do you think that unhappiness will last? They themselves do not know. They might find joy after crying.

The daily life of a human being centered around their surroundings is like that. Daily life weaves such stories. Not just for a day, but looking through hundreds or thousands of generations, some tribes may be happy, and some may be blessed, but when viewed over tens of thousands or hundreds of thousands of years, that cannot be guaranteed.

If there are ten thousand people in a happy place, is there anyone among them who would want to be in an unhappy place? "No." Not a single person, but they can be driven into unhappiness all at once without mercy.

When viewed this way, if someone becomes the president of the United States today, they might think they are the happiest person in the world. The president of the United States might think they are happier than anyone else, but can they guarantee that this country, which is like this now, will always be in a glorious position to lead the world in a century or two? Can they guarantee that? "I can make it happen. I am a Harvard student, and I can do it with my power," can they say that?

For example, let’s say there is a man who does whatever he wants. If someone says that, they are speaking within a certain limit. What does that mean? It means they are speaking within the realm of influence they can exert. Everything is like that. Can such a person say, "Hey, sun! I am busy this morning, so don't rise on time, rise an hour late"? Can they do that? "No." That would be a madman. A madman. (Laughter) And if they say, "I have to go on a business trip today, so clouds, don't gather. It can't rain. Even if the weather forecast says this, throw it away and do it my way," will that work? How limited are we? Looking at that, we cannot absolutely control the environmental conditions in any place.

You cannot control the seasons at will. You cannot cook a day as you please. Can you say to your nose, "Hey, nose! What are you busy with? Why are you doing this? Breathe only one-third of the time"? Can you say to your blinking eyes, "Hey, blink only one-tenth of the time. I am busy, and it's a disturbance"? And can you say to your hair, "Hey, why do you keep growing? The Munni are busy cutting. Once a year is enough; why do you keep growing? Stop!" Can you control even your hair? You cannot control even a single hair. Can you control it? "No."

Since you cannot control the environment, you cannot control the movements and actions of the universe either. Therefore, wise people, especially those who pursue happiness, should not try to conquer the environment. There are only two methods: overcoming the environment and following the environment. The path that a wise person should choose
Now, as I talk about this, an hour has already passed. I have little time left. When looking at this, a wise person is someone who decides to go through the difficult path while holding onto hope for the future, while a foolish person is someone who throws away the dream of the future for immediate happiness.

Everyone knows the story of the grasshopper and the ant, right? So, will you be a grasshopper or an ant? "An ant." These days, women are dieting to slim down their waists, right? Oh, you guys! Heavenly fortune and destiny
I believe you all have been quite shocked by the sudden passing of President Park due to an accidental incident. I ask that you, members of the Unification Church, remain calm and composed, and dedicate your sincerity to heaven. While praying for the repose of the deceased, I ask that you also be mindful of the future situation of this country.

The brief topic I want to discuss is "Heavenly Fortune and Destiny." Let's talk about this for a moment.

Everything moves according to the laws of heaven and earth. When we look at the four seasons, a year moves according to those seasons. Even in a single day, there is a morning like spring, a daytime like summer, an evening like autumn, and a night like winter. We know that all of this follows the orderly path of heaven and earth, circulating and developing in repetition.

The fate of human beings living in such a natural environment is no different. There is a childhood stage, followed by a youth stage, then a middle age stage, and finally an old age stage. Through such processes, we walk the path of life. The fate of a nation is the same.

The fate of a nation sometimes faces difficult times, like winter, but from those circumstances, it gains new life and goes through a growing period like spring, then a process like summer, followed by a maturing period like autumn, and finally meets winter. Just as the fate of a nation moves according to the laws of heaven and earth, we can imagine that the rise and fall of all nations in history follows a similar path.

No individual, family, or nation wishes to perish forever, to develop, or to prosper, but they all encounter the phenomenon of reaching a limit, like the arrival of autumn. We have seen this repeated many times throughout history.

When we look at all the processes that pass, after one season passes, a new season comes. In this process, spring is not always the same spring. Summer is not always the same summer. We can see that various living conditions and circumstances change even within that summer.

The development of cultural worlds is the same. There are spring civilizations, summer civilizations, autumn civilizations, and winter civilizations. Ancient civilizations began from summer civilizations. For instance, Egyptian civilization, the Yellow River civilization in ancient China, and ancient Indian civilization all started from summer civilizations within the tropical zone. Modern 20th-century civilization has transitioned into temperate zone civilization.

In contrast, the communist forces have spread their influence from the north, blowing cold winds against beings that lack the essence of all divine and life content. It is like the cold winds of winter, with snow swirling around. Then, the leaves all fall, and even the bare branches that have nothing die and break. If one lacks vitality, no matter how large a tree is, it will inevitably face its end.

What remains in that winter? Only those trees or branches standing on a foundation that possesses vitality will survive.

Heavenly fortune goes through long cycles of rise and fall.
So, when we look at God's providence regarding the cultural world today, what is it for? It is to leave behind the final point of culture that possesses life. Today, whether it is Christianity or many other religions that have developed throughout history, the ultimate position of those developed denominations is a matter of whether they remain as entities that possess life.

From this perspective, no matter how strong the wind blows, how difficult the environment is, or how harsh the winter storms come, as long as there is life, it will overcome that environment. Once it overcomes, what happens? It connects to new life in spring and develops further.

When we look at people, they are all different. Some are born in the summer, some in autumn, some in winter, and some in spring. Those born in the spring carry the vitality of spring and go through the summer in their life journey. Those born in such a position can live well throughout their lives. They are born in good conditions and can flourish without envying anyone.

Some start in the summer and disappear in the autumn. Those born in the middle of summer may have a good summer, but they gradually head toward autumn. Some are born in winter. Their birth may be unfortunate and they may suffer, but when they overcome the winter, a time like spring will come when they can revive. 

When we look at the fate and path of all people, they are all different. Person A, Person B, Person C are all different. That person is so happy, but why am I so unhappy? This is because when we look at the current existence of human beings, we tend to cut and view it from that perspective, labeling it as happiness or unhappiness. However, when we consider the laws of heaven and earth, when we look at the system of one year, winter is not bad, and spring is not good. Autumn is not good, and summer is not bad either. All can be good, forming a realm of life and operating accordingly. 

From our limited perspective, when we cut it, it may seem like a miserable fact or a difficult reality, but when we see it as a whole, it may be necessary for connecting the entirety. This is something to think about.

In the history of restoration, God has not been able to act as God until now. What kind of God is a God who cannot save sinners? A God who seeks to save sinners is a God of suffering and tribulation. He has not become a God of glory. The God who faced fallen human ancestors is a God of misery, despair, and a heart full of pain.

Where can we find a God who can proclaim liberation, pride, and praise? Is it good for a sick person to have a nation and a people? It is the same. There is no separate way to heal a sickness. You must take medicine. Medicine is originally bitter. Right? We must find Cain.

So what should we do? We must find the parents. To return to the parents, what must we do? The younger brother must... The lost one is the older brother, but when seeking, the older brother becomes the younger brother, and the parents of the world... it becomes the opposite. Do you understand? A historical revolution must unfold. The older brother follows the younger brother, the mother follows behind the older brother, and the father follows behind the mother.

This miserable history of losing parents, because we lost God, we must find the position to host God again, centered on God's will, representing Abel, and we must find the older brother—those who were first fallen, those who first became evil in the world of Satan—and place them in the position of the younger brother. The older brother must take the place of the younger brother. Can such a thing happen in the world? It is because of this that Jacob engaged in the game of buying the birthright from his brother. He laid the foundation of reality centered on that condition. Do you understand what I mean? 

If I am in the position of Abel, the Republic of Korea must follow from the position of Cain. To make the Republic of Korea follow, we cannot just say, "Republic of Korea, follow me!" We must stand in a place of repentance where the nation sheds tears, saying, "I will not go first; you must go first." Without that, we cannot go.

What is the fall in Eden? It is the fight between Cain and Abel, but Cain was born as the older brother. Abel was born as the younger brother. This is the grudge. We must turn this around. Without doing so, there is no way to find the parents. In the providence of God that has walked through such a convoluted history, what does the Unification Church claim today? It is home church. 

What is the Garden of Eden? It is home church. Do you understand? There is no fight between Cain and Abel, the older brother and the younger brother. Thus, they become one with the parents, and God and the archangel become one, and everything becomes one and unified. For this environment, today, Reverend Moon is coming out to break down the boundaries between the angelic world and heaven, and the boundaries between the human world and the angelic world, and to break down the walls of enmity between Cain and Abel and correct this.

So, what is home church? What is family church? It is to abandon all borders and social systems centered on the providence of all historical eras and to restore everything by becoming one within the family church. Do you understand? 

The 360 families are 360 tribes. Why do we do that? Because 36 is three times 12. Isn't that right? The number 12 represents the way of heaven. This refers to the twelve pearl gates of the spirit world. It is similar to the number of 36 families. It can connect the three stages of fortune from the Old Testament, New Testament, and the Age of the Holy Testament. This has all come out to resolve salvation.

Centered on the word 360, a day of 360 days represents a day of eternity. To find a home church in that perspective is a game to establish many days of victory before God in this historical era. The 360 families are for recovering what humanity could not establish in the heavenly kingdom and the days of victory. It is a game to establish 360 days before God, and the 360 families are for humanity to have. Therefore, the 360 families are necessary. It is a day of hope, not a day of sorrow. No matter how hard it is, we must go for hope. It is possible.

To become one with the older brother and serve the parents is the ideal heavenly kingdom. The Unification Church has been persecuted until now, but now that we have overcome all that, there is no need for teachers like me to shed blood and sweat. Even if we shed tears, we do so with gratitude, and even if we sweat, we do so with gratitude; it is all gratitude. Even while suffering greatly, it is only gratitude. Even while being insulted, we are grateful. We digest everything.

What kind of people go to hell on this earth? They are people who go because they are sad, people who go because they are lonely, people who go because they are discouraged. They go while crying. They do not go while laughing. There are tens of billions of people who have gone like that.

What can digest the groans of despair with laughter? It is the family church. Do you understand? Family is home, and church is the church. That is why when you return, you must return to your hometown. You must return to your mother and father. You must return to your mother and father and carry out the home church movement.

Reverend Moon has never been able to talk about the Principle to his parents until now. The older brother was connected to the spirit world and was a person of good faith. He was someone who prayed and healed his wife who was terminally ill. He is the older brother who loved me more than anyone. Yet, he could not talk about the Principle. He cannot give something precious to his own clan. If God could give something precious to His beloved clan, He would not have raised righteous people on this earth to sacrifice them. Because there is a path of salvation that the older brother in the position of Cain must take... Because loving Cain is to love the brother, it is a path of salvation, and we cannot love by violating that path.

To establish the kingdom of God, we must set the condition of love that has been loved. When that condition is established, Satan retreats before salvation. We must govern with salvation. Therefore, we must inevitably put all those who have been working for heaven until now in a position of death. Why? Because there is salvation. Love those who were born as older brothers, love the brothers... The younger brother is better. So, since the younger brother is better, when thinking of saving the older brother, it is a happy thing to consider him as a sacrifice. Therefore, we must sacrifice well.

So how must we find the parents? Before finding the parents, the brothers must first become one; otherwise, it is absolutely impossible. That is why we are going globally. The democratic world is Abel-like, and the communist world is Cain-like. Therefore, America must subjugate the Soviet Union. Before loving humanity, we must love the communists more and make the communists follow America. 

When that happens, we will be able to host God as the universal parent. Then God's love will reign on this earth. On that day, having received God's love, we will love our brothers and will not even fight if told to. What is the use of fighting? How tiresome is it to have fallen from the Garden of Eden? How tiresome is the path of bloodshed from fighting in the Garden of Eden until now? An individual cannot go to heaven alone. We must come together, become one with the older brother, and serve the parents. We must bring the parents. One cannot serve the parents alone. Right?

What is indemnity restoration? It is to unite what has been divided. Many nations and diverse races have all been divided, so we must gather them. Therefore, what the teacher does is to unite the diverse races centered on love. We lay the foundation to connect all families through the Cain lineage and the Abel lineage. By placing them in the position of parents, we can finally enter heaven...

We must enter with God on the foundation that can host God in a victorious foundation. We must enter with God; can one enter heaven alone? Even Jesus could only go as far as paradise, right? Therefore, if we cannot do home church now, you will absolutely not be able to go to heaven. The heaven of the past has been the restored heaven, the restored heaven. Those who are in the restored heaven must return to this earth to fulfill indemnity to go to the ideal heaven. We on earth are going to the restored heaven. (The following words could not be recorded due to poor recording conditions.) *
